In [3]:
import urllib.request
from io import BytesIO

# Replace the URL below with your actual remote PDF file URL
remote_pdf_url = "https://tessarinseve.pythonanywhere.com/staticweb/calendar2024.pdf"

# Fetch the PDF content
pdf_bytes = urllib.request.urlopen(remote_pdf_url).read()

# Create a BytesIO object with the PDF data
pdf_buffer = BytesIO(pdf_bytes)
In [7]:
WIDTH, HEIGHT = 800, 400 
from base64 import b64encode
from IPython.display import display, HTML
base64_pdf = b64encode(pdf_bytes).decode("utf-8")
display(HTML(f'<embed src="data:application/pdf;base64,{base64_pdf} width= {WIDTH} height={HEIGHT} type=application/pdf>'))

import fitz  # PyMuPDF
from IPython.display import HTML

# Replace 'your-pdf-file.pdf' with the actual path to your PDF file
pdf_path = remote_pdf_url

# Read the PDF and convert it to HTML
doc = fitz.open(stream=pdf_buffer)
doc.page_count
page = doc[0]
pdf_html = page.get_textpage()
HTML(pdf_html.extractHTML())
